The Refusal--Compliance Tradeoff: A Large-Scale Safety Behavior Audit of Large Language Models
Authors: Alif Al Hasan, Sumon Biswas
First: 2026-05-06T20:35:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-30T15:07:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Refusal rates are a poor proxy for LLM safety, i.e., a model may over-refuse benign prompts while still complying with harmful ones. We audit both failure modes across 21 open-weight LLMs on four safety benchmarks (OR-Bench, XSTest, ToxiGen, BOLD), using a composition adjustment to isolate model sensitivity from dataset toxicity confounds. We report three findings. First, models adopt fundamentally different calibration strategies: conservative ecosystems such as Llama suppress unsafe outputs at the cost of elevated over-refusals, while permissive ecosystems such as DeepSeek and Qwen preserve helpfulness but tolerate higher harmful compliance. Second, demographic protection is unequal: models over-protect prominent racial and religious groups, frequently refusing even benign prompts about them, while providing substantially weaker protection against disability-targeted attacks. Third, refusal and compliance tendencies are stable within model families across generations and scales, suggesting that post-training objectives shape safety behavior more than architecture. Our results call for joint, demographically-aware, and multi-judge safety evaluation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：拒绝与合规权衡：大规模语言模型的安全行为审计
拒绝率是大型语言模型安全性的一个糟糕代理，即模型可能在拒绝良性提示的同时仍然对有害提示做出反应。我们在四个安全基准（OR-Bench、XSTest、ToxiGen、BOLD）上审计了21个开放权重的大型语言模型的这两种失败模式，使用组合调整来隔离模型敏感性与数据集毒性混淆。我们报告了三项发现。首先，模型采用根本不同的校准策略：保守生态系统如Llama在提高过度拒绝的代价下抑制不安全输出，而宽松生态系统如DeepSeek和Qwen则保持有用性但容忍更高的有害合规性。其次，人口保护不平等：模型过度保护显著的种族和宗教群体，常常拒绝关于它们的良性提示，而对残疾目标攻击提供的保护则明显较弱。第三，拒绝和合规倾向在模型家族中跨代和规模保持稳定，表明后训练目标在塑造安全行为方面的影响大于架构。我们的结果呼吁进行联合、关注人口统计和多评审的安全评估。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the inadequacy of refusal rates as indicators of safety in large language models (LLMs), highlighting that models may refuse benign prompts while complying with harmful ones. Previous methods primarily focused on refusal rates without considering the nuances of model behavior, leading to misleading assessments of safety. The proposed approach involves a large-scale audit of 21 open-weight LLMs across four safety benchmarks, utilizing a composition adjustment to differentiate model sensitivity from dataset toxicity. The study contributes by revealing distinct calibration strategies among models, unequal demographic protection, and the stability of refusal and compliance tendencies across model families, suggesting that post-training objectives significantly influence safety behavior. The methodology demonstrates that models like Llama prioritize safety at the expense of over-refusals, while others maintain helpfulness but allow harmful compliance, thus providing a more comprehensive understanding of LLM safety behavior.
本研究探讨了拒绝率作为大型语言模型（LLMs）安全性指标的不足，强调模型可能拒绝良性提示而对有害提示却予以遵从。以往的方法主要关注拒绝率，而未考虑模型行为的细微差别，导致对安全性的误导性评估。所提出的方法涉及对21个开放权重的LLM进行审计，使用四个安全基准，并采用组合调整以区分模型敏感性与数据集毒性。该方法揭示了模型表现出不同的校准策略，保守模型如Llama优先考虑安全性，但导致过度拒绝，而宽容模型如DeepSeek则保持有用性，但允许有害遵从。研究贡献在于理解模型保护中的人口差异，并表明安全行为更多地受到后训练目标的影响，而非架构。研究结果强调了需要一个全面的、考虑人口因素的安全评估框架。
How Reliable Are AI Attackers Against a Fixed Vulnerable Target? A 400-Run Empirical Study of LLM Penetration Testing Consistency
Authors: Galip Tolga Erdem
First: 2026-05-28T15:39:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-28T15:39:43+00:00
Comments: 41 pages, 7 figures. Code and 400-run dataset: https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.20421592
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) can autonomously conduct multi-stage cyber attacks, but the consistency of their offensive behavior under repeated trials remains unstudied. This work presents the first large-scale empirical measurement of LLM attack consistency: 400 autonomous penetration testing runs (4 models, 100 each) against an identical honeypot hosting OWASP Juice Shop and two additional vulnerable services, holding prompt, orchestrator, and target constant. No model emitted a content refusal that survived the orchestrator's one-shot authorization re-prompt at iterations 0-1. Claude Sonnet 4's API calls did encounter upstream service unavailability - 91 of 1,135 calls returned HTTP 529 overloaded_error during a documented Anthropic capacity event, truncating 39 of 100 Claude runs. An earlier draft catalogued these as safety refusals; on full-log audit they are upstream API failures, not model-level refusals. Despite this, Claude achieved full exploitation in 61 of 100 runs; Gemini 2.5 Flash-Lite in 85; GPT-4o-mini in 56 while deploying 98 unique attack strategies; qwen2.5-coder:14b in 25. Failure modes are model-distinctive: Claude through API truncation (39 runs), qwen through premature completion (52), GPT-4o-mini through iteration-budget exhaustion (23). Cross-service credential reuse appeared only in configurations retaining the most conversation history (qwen 57%, GPT-4o-mini 49%, cloud models 0% on 5-exchange windows). Cross-model exploitation rate differences are statistically significant (p < 0.001) with large effect sizes; qwen vs. Gemini SQL injection rates differ at Cohen's h = 1.12. First-exploit timing fell within a 15-30 second wall-clock range. To our knowledge, this is the first study to measure autonomous LLM attack behavior at N=100 per model across a multi-service target.
中文标题/摘要
标题：人工智能攻击者对固定脆弱目标的可靠性如何？一项关于大型语言模型渗透测试一致性的400次实证研究
大型语言模型（LLMs）可以自主进行多阶段网络攻击，但其在重复试验中的攻击行为一致性尚未研究。本研究首次大规模实证测量LLM攻击一致性：对一个托管OWASP Juice Shop和两个额外脆弱服务的相同蜜罐进行400次自主渗透测试（4个模型，各100次），保持提示、协调者和目标不变。在迭代0-1中，没有模型发出经过协调者一次性授权重新提示后仍然有效的内容拒绝。Claude Sonnet 4的API调用确实遇到了上游服务不可用的情况——在一次记录的Anthropic容量事件中，1,135次调用中有91次返回HTTP 529 overloaded_error，截断了100次Claude运行中的39次。早期草稿将这些列为安全拒绝；经过完整日志审计后，它们被认定为上游API故障，而非模型级拒绝。尽管如此，Claude在100次运行中实现了61次完全利用；Gemini 2.5 Flash-Lite为85次；GPT-4o-mini为56次，同时部署了98种独特的攻击策略；qwen2.5-coder:14b为25次。失败模式具有模型特征：Claude通过API截断（39次运行），qwen通过过早完成（52次），GPT-4o-mini通过迭代预算耗尽（23次）。跨服务凭证重用仅出现在保留最多对话历史的配置中（qwen 57%，GPT-4o-mini 49%，云模型在5次交换窗口中为0%）。跨模型利用率差异具有统计显著性（p < 0.001），且效应量较大；qwen与Gemini的SQL注入率差异为Cohen's h = 1.12。首次利用的时间落在15-30秒的实际时间范围内。据我们所知，这是首个在多服务目标上对每个模型进行N=100的自主LLM攻击行为测量的研究。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the gap in understanding the consistency of large language models (LLMs) in conducting cyber attacks, as previous studies have not empirically measured their offensive behavior across multiple trials. Traditional methods lacked comprehensive analysis and did not account for variations in model performance under repeated conditions. The proposed approach involves a large-scale empirical study consisting of 400 autonomous penetration testing runs across four different LLMs targeting a uniform honeypot environment, allowing for a direct comparison of their attack strategies and success rates. The findings reveal significant differences in exploitation rates and failure modes among the models, with Claude achieving full exploitation in 61% of runs and qwen2.5-coder:14b in only 25%, highlighting the distinct behaviors of each model. This study contributes to the field by providing the first empirical evidence of LLM attack consistency, demonstrating that cross-model exploitation rates are statistically significant and offering insights into the reliability of AI attackers against fixed vulnerable targets.
本研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）在进行多阶段网络攻击时的一致性，这是一个尚未被研究的领域。过去的方法缺乏对攻击一致性的实证测量，导致对LLMs在渗透测试中可靠性的疑虑。所提出的方法涉及对四个模型在固定蜜罐上进行的400次自主渗透测试的实证研究，保持条件不变。研究表明，尽管没有模型在协调者的重新提示下表现出内容拒绝，但某些运行受到API不可用性的影响，这在早期草稿中被误分类为模型拒绝。结果显示模型之间的利用率存在显著差异，Claude在61%的运行中实现了完全利用，而qwen2.5-coder:14b仅为25%，突显了不同的失败模式和跨服务凭据重用模式。这项工作有助于理解LLM攻击行为，并为未来的人工智能网络安全研究奠定了基础。
Beyond Attack Success Rate: Temporal Logit Observability for LLM Safety Failures
Authors: Junyoung Park, Sunghwan Park, Seongyong Ju, Jaewoo Lee
First: 2026-05-28T09:02:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-28T09:02:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Attack Success Rate (ASR) evaluates each jailbreak with a single yes/no label at the end of generation, telling us whether a failure happened but not how it unfolded. Two attacks that produce equally harmful outputs may have followed completely different paths, and ASR cannot tell them apart. We make those hidden paths observable from logits alone. Temporal Logit Observability (TLO) is a training-free diagnostic that watches a compliance-refusal margin during decoding and places each model-attack condition on a calibrated 2D plane. By design, this plane is most informative exactly where ASR is least informative: among attacks that succeed for genuinely different reasons. Across four aligned LLMs and three jailbreak paradigms, attacks with nearly identical ASR land at clearly different points on the plane: the same model can fail through different temporal patterns. The geometry matches refusal-direction probes from hidden states on most conditions, with one model showing the limit of our fixed-lexicon approach. A simple early-stop rule derived from TLO cuts successful jailbreaks by more than half, without false alarms on plain benign queries. Safety evaluation should report when and how a failure unfolds, not only whether it occurred. TLO makes the first two observable from logits alone.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越攻击成功率：大型语言模型安全失败的时间逻辑可观察性
攻击成功率（ASR）在生成结束时用单一的是/否标签评估每个越狱，告诉我们是否发生了失败，但无法说明其过程。两个产生同样有害输出的攻击可能遵循完全不同的路径，而ASR无法区分它们。我们使这些隐藏路径仅通过逻辑可观察。时间逻辑可观察性（TLO）是一种无训练的诊断方法，在解码过程中观察合规-拒绝边际，并将每个模型-攻击条件放置在一个校准的二维平面上。根据设计，这个平面在ASR信息最少的地方最具信息性：在因真正不同原因而成功的攻击之间。在四个对齐的大型语言模型和三种越狱范式中，攻击的ASR几乎相同，但在平面上明显位于不同点：同一模型可以通过不同的时间模式失败。几何形状与大多数条件下隐藏状态的拒绝方向探测相匹配，其中一个模型显示了我们固定词汇表方法的极限。基于TLO的简单早停规则将成功的越狱减少了一半以上，而在普通良性查询上没有误报。安全评估应报告失败何时以及如何发生，而不仅仅是是否发生。TLO使前两者仅通过逻辑可观察。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the limitations of the Attack Success Rate (ASR) metric, which only indicates whether a jailbreak attack on large language models (LLMs) was successful without revealing the underlying processes. Previous methods have focused solely on ASR, failing to differentiate between attacks that yield similar harmful outputs but follow different paths. The proposed Temporal Logit Observability (TLO) method offers a training-free diagnostic approach that visualizes the compliance-refusal margin during decoding, allowing for a more nuanced understanding of model failures. This method contributes to the field by enabling the observation of how failures occur, rather than just if they occur, and demonstrates that attacks with identical ASR can be distinguished based on their temporal patterns. The methodology was tested across four aligned LLMs and three jailbreak paradigms, resulting in a significant reduction of successful jailbreaks by over half while maintaining accuracy on benign queries, thus supporting the goal of improving LLM safety evaluations.
本研究解决了攻击成功率（ASR）指标的局限性，该指标仅指示大型语言模型（LLM）上的越狱攻击是否成功，而未提供这些失败的潜在过程的见解。以往的方法依赖于ASR，无法区分可能产生相似有害输出但路径不同的攻击。提出的方法，时间逻辑可观察性（TLO），提供了一种无训练的诊断方法，通过在解码过程中可视化合规-拒绝边际，绘制出一个经过校准的二维平面，从而揭示攻击的隐藏路径。该方法的动机明确，因为它通过展示失败发生的方式和时间，增强了对LLM安全失败的理解。论文表明，TLO能够有效区分在四个对齐的LLM和三种越狱范式下具有相同ASR的攻击，通过简单的提前停止规则将成功越狱的数量减少了一半以上，从而支持了通过提供对失败机制的更深入见解来改善LLM安全评估的目标。
Aligned but Fragile: Enhancing LLM Safety Robustness via Zeroth-Order Optimization
Authors: Zhihao Liu, Yifan Wu, Jian Lou, Di Wang, Yuxi Zhou, Yuke Hu
First: 2026-05-28T05:46:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-28T05:46:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety alignment for large language models (LLMs) aims to reduce harmful or unsafe behavior while preserving general utility. However, recent findings reveal that alignment effects can be fragile: lightweight post-alignment manipulations, such as parameter noise, activation noise, or quantization, can easily weaken the intended safety behavior. Prior efforts to improve robustness have primarily focused on data curation, modified alignment objectives, and safety-critical parameter identification, leaving the role of the optimizer itself largely unexplored. In this paper, we are the first to study the robustness of safety alignment from the perspective of the base optimizer. This optimizer-centric view naturally points to zeroth-order optimization, which provides a robustness-oriented signal by evaluating safety alignment under perturbations. Based on this insight, we propose a hybrid framework that first performs standard first-order safety alignment and then applies zeroth-order refinement to improve robustness. Both theoretically and empirically, we show that only a few zeroth-order refinement steps can enhance robustness while preserving safety alignment. We further improve the efficiency of zeroth-order refinement by exploiting its inherent perturbation-based evaluations to estimate layer-wise robustness sensitivity, enabling the refinement process to concentrate updates on robustness-critical layers with modest training overhead.
中文标题/摘要
标题：对齐但脆弱：通过零阶优化增强大型语言模型的安全性鲁棒性
大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全对齐旨在减少有害或不安全行为，同时保持一般效用。然而，最近的研究发现，对齐效果可能是脆弱的：轻量级的后对齐操作，如参数噪声、激活噪声或量化，可能会轻易削弱预期的安全行为。以往提高鲁棒性的努力主要集中在数据策划、修改对齐目标和安全关键参数识别上，而优化器本身的作用则大多未被探索。 在本文中，我们首次从基础优化器的角度研究安全对齐的鲁棒性。这种以优化器为中心的视角自然指向零阶优化，它通过在扰动下评估安全对齐提供了一个面向鲁棒性的信号。基于这一见解，我们提出了一个混合框架，首先执行标准的一阶安全对齐，然后应用零阶精炼以提高鲁棒性。我们理论和实证地表明，仅需少量零阶精炼步骤即可在保持安全对齐的同时增强鲁棒性。我们进一步通过利用零阶精炼固有的基于扰动的评估来估计层级鲁棒性敏感性，提高了零阶精炼的效率，使精炼过程能够将更新集中在鲁棒性关键层上，且训练开销适中。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the challenge of safety alignment in large language models (LLMs), which aims to mitigate harmful behaviors while maintaining utility. Previous methods have primarily focused on data curation and modified alignment objectives, but they often overlook the optimizer's role, leading to fragile safety alignment that can be easily disrupted by minor perturbations. This paper proposes a novel approach that centers on zeroth-order optimization, enhancing robustness by evaluating safety alignment under perturbations. The methodology involves a hybrid framework that combines standard first-order safety alignment with zeroth-order refinement, demonstrating that minimal refinement steps can significantly improve robustness without compromising safety alignment. The experimental results indicate that this approach effectively concentrates updates on critical layers, achieving improved robustness while maintaining efficiency.
本研究解决了大型语言模型（LLMs）中安全对齐的挑战，旨在减轻有害行为，同时保持整体效用。以往的方法主要集中在数据整理和修改对齐目标上，但往往忽视了优化器的作用，导致安全对齐脆弱，容易受到微小扰动的影响。本文提出了一种新颖的方法，聚焦于零阶优化，以增强安全对齐的鲁棒性，将标准的一阶安全对齐与零阶精炼相结合。该方法论表明，最少的零阶精炼步骤可以显著提高鲁棒性，而不损害安全对齐，且实现了对关键层的高效更新。实验结果表明，该混合框架有效增强了安全对齐对扰动的抵抗力，支持了鲁棒LLM安全的目标。
SelfGrader: LLM Jailbreak Detection via Anchored Token-Level Logits
Authors: Zikai Zhang, Rui Hu, Olivera Kotevska, Jiahao Xu
First: 2026-04-01T23:29:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-28T05:44:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) are powerful tools for answering user queries, yet they remain highly vulnerable to jailbreak attacks. Existing guardrail methods typically rely on internal features or textual responses to detect malicious queries, which either introduce substantial latency or suffer from randomness in text generation. To overcome these limitations, we propose SelfGrader, a lightweight guardrail method that formulates jailbreak detection as a numerical grading problem using anchored token-level logits. Specifically, SelfGrader evaluates the safety of a user query within a compact set of numerical tokens (NTs) (e.g., 0-9) and interprets their logit distribution as an internal safety signal. To align these signals with the target safety rubric, SelfGrader constructs Probably Approximately Correct-guided ICL anchor examples and introduces a dual-perspective scoring rule that considers both the maliciousness and benignness of the query, yielding a stable and interpretable score that reflects harmfulness and reduces the false positive rate simultaneously. Extensive experiments across diverse jailbreak benchmarks, adaptive attacks, benign prompt benchmarks, multiple LLMs, and state-of-the-art guardrail baselines demonstrate that SelfGrader achieves strong robustness with low false positive rates, memory overhead, and latency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SelfGrader：通过锚定的令牌级逻辑进行LLM越狱检测
大型语言模型（LLMs）是回答用户查询的强大工具，但它们仍然高度易受越狱攻击。现有的防护方法通常依赖于内部特征或文本响应来检测恶意查询，这要么引入了显著的延迟，要么在文本生成中遭受随机性。为克服这些限制，我们提出了SelfGrader，这是一种轻量级的防护方法，将越狱检测公式化为使用锚定令牌级逻辑的数值评分问题。具体而言，SelfGrader在一组紧凑的数值令牌（NTs）（例如，0-9）中评估用户查询的安全性，并将其逻辑分布解释为内部安全信号。为了将这些信号与目标安全标准对齐，SelfGrader构建了可能近似正确指导的ICL锚定示例，并引入了一种双视角评分规则，考虑查询的恶意性和良性，从而产生一个稳定且可解释的分数，反映有害性并同时降低误报率。在多种越狱基准、适应性攻击、良性提示基准、多个LLM和最先进的防护基线上的广泛实验表明，SelfGrader在低误报率、内存开销和延迟方面实现了强大的鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the vulnerability of Large Language Models (LLMs) to jailbreak attacks, highlighting the limitations of existing guardrail methods that rely on internal features or textual responses, which can introduce latency and randomness. The proposed approach, SelfGrader, differs by framing jailbreak detection as a numerical grading problem using anchored token-level logits, which allows for a more stable and interpretable assessment of query safety. The contribution of this paper lies in its innovative method that utilizes Probably Approximately Correct-guided ICL anchor examples and a dual-perspective scoring rule to evaluate both malicious and benign queries, effectively reducing false positive rates. The methodology involves evaluating user queries through a compact set of numerical tokens and interpreting their logit distribution as a safety signal, achieving strong robustness across various benchmarks with low memory overhead and latency, thus supporting the goal of enhancing LLM security.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLM）对越狱攻击的脆弱性，指出现有检测方法通常依赖内部特征或文本响应，这可能导致延迟或随机性。所提出的方法SelfGrader通过将越狱检测框架化为使用锚定的令牌级logits的数值评分问题，从而实现了更高效的用户查询评估。这种方法具有良好的动机，旨在提供稳定且可解释的安全信号，同时减少误报率。该方法论包括构建概率近似正确引导的ICL锚定示例，并采用双视角评分规则，评估查询的恶意和良性方面。实验结果表明，SelfGrader在各种基准测试中表现出强大的鲁棒性，具有低误报率、内存开销和延迟，有效支持其增强LLM安全性的目标。
Jailbreaking and Mitigation of Vulnerabilities in Large Language Models
Authors: Benji Peng, Hanxuan Chen, Keyu Chen, Qian Niu, Ziqian Bi, Ming Liu, Pohsun Feng, Tianyang Wang, Lawrence K. Q. Yan, Yizhu Wen, Yichao Zhang, Caitlyn Heqi Yin, Xinyuan Song, Riyang Bao, Jiacheng Shi
Venue: Eureka 1(1) (2026) 26-61
First: 2024-10-20T00:00:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-27T16:38:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have transformed artificial intelligence by advancing natural language understanding and generation, enabling applications across fields beyond healthcare, software engineering, and conversational systems. Despite these advancements in the past few years, LLMs have shown considerable vulnerabilities, particularly to prompt injection and jailbreaking attacks. This review analyzes the state of research on these vulnerabilities and presents available defense strategies. We roughly categorize attack approaches into prompt-based, model-based, multimodal, and multilingual, covering techniques such as adversarial prompting, backdoor injections, and cross-modality exploits. We also review various defense mechanisms, including prompt filtering, transformation, alignment techniques, multi-agent defenses, and self-regulation, evaluating their strengths and shortcomings. We also discuss key metrics and benchmarks used to assess LLM safety and robustness, noting challenges like the quantification of attack success in interactive contexts and biases in existing datasets. Identifying current research gaps, we suggest future directions for resilient alignment strategies, advanced defenses against evolving attacks, automation of jailbreak detection, and consideration of ethical and societal impacts. This review emphasizes the need for continued research and cooperation within the AI community to enhance LLM security and ensure their safe deployment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大型语言模型的越狱与漏洞缓解
大型语言模型（LLMs）通过推动自然语言理解和生成，改变了人工智能，使其在医疗、软件工程和对话系统等多个领域的应用成为可能。尽管近年来取得了这些进展，LLMs仍显示出相当大的脆弱性，特别是对提示注入和越狱攻击。本文回顾了这些漏洞的研究现状，并提出了可用的防御策略。我们大致将攻击方法分为基于提示、基于模型、多模态和多语言，涵盖对抗性提示、后门注入和跨模态利用等技术。我们还回顾了各种防御机制，包括提示过滤、转换、对齐技术、多智能体防御和自我调节，评估其优缺点。我们讨论了用于评估LLM安全性和鲁棒性的关键指标和基准，指出了在交互环境中量化攻击成功率和现有数据集中的偏见等挑战。识别当前研究空白，我们建议未来在弹性对齐策略、针对不断演变的攻击的高级防御、越狱检测的自动化以及伦理和社会影响的考虑等方面的研究方向。本文强调了在AI社区内持续研究和合作的必要性，以增强LLM安全性并确保其安全部署。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the significant vulnerabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs), particularly their susceptibility to prompt injection and jailbreaking attacks, which pose risks across various applications. Previous methods of defense, such as prompt filtering and transformation, have shown limitations in effectively mitigating these vulnerabilities, necessitating a more comprehensive approach. This paper contributes by categorizing attack strategies and defense mechanisms, evaluating their effectiveness, and identifying gaps in current research. The proposed methodology involves a thorough review of existing vulnerabilities and defenses, alongside suggestions for future research directions aimed at enhancing LLM security. The findings highlight the need for improved alignment strategies and advanced defenses, ultimately supporting the goal of ensuring safe deployment of LLMs in diverse fields.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）在面对各种攻击（如提示注入和越狱）时的显著脆弱性，尽管这些模型在自然语言处理方面取得了进展。以往的防御方法，如提示过滤和多代理防御，显示出在有效性和适应性方面的局限性。本文提出对现有攻击策略和防御机制的全面回顾，强调它们的优缺点，同时识别当前研究中的空白。该方法论包括对攻击方法的分类和对防御策略的评估，最终建议未来在提高LLM安全性方面的方向。研究结果表明，迫切需要增强的对齐策略和稳健的防御，强调了持续研究以确保LLM在多种应用中安全部署的重要性。
Got a Secret? LLM Agents Can't Keep It: Evaluating Privacy in Multi-Agent Systems
Authors: Aman Priyanshu, Supriti Vijay, Esha Pahwa
First: 2026-05-26T23:32:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-26T23:32:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
LLM safety evaluations predominantly test models in isolation, yet deployed AI agents increasingly operate within persistent social environments alongside other agents. We introduce a Moltbook-style simulation platform where thousands of LLM agents interact across communities over a simulated month, and use it to evaluate privacy as a downstream safety concern under varying degrees of social pressure. We find that shifting from single turn to multi turn social evaluation amplifies privacy violations (CIMemories 19.95% to Ours 45.30% across OpenAI models), that leakage is socially contagious, with agents 8 times more likely to disclose sensitive information after observing a peer do so, and that explicit privacy instructions reduce but do not eliminate this effect, leaving leakage rates above 37.8% even with safeguards. Our findings suggest that static chat based safety benchmarks systematically underestimate risks in agentic deployment, and that social context alone is sufficient to elicit sensitive disclosures that single turn evaluations would never surface.
中文标题/摘要
标题：有秘密吗？LLM代理无法保守秘密：多代理系统中的隐私评估
LLM安全评估主要在孤立环境中测试模型，但部署的AI代理越来越多地在与其他代理的持久社交环境中操作。我们引入了一种Moltbook风格的模拟平台，在该平台上，数千个LLM代理在模拟的一个月内跨社区互动，并利用它评估在不同社交压力下的隐私作为下游安全问题。我们发现，从单轮到多轮社交评估的转变会加剧隐私侵犯（CIMemories 19.95%到我们的模型45.30%），泄露具有社交传染性，代理在观察到同伴泄露后泄露敏感信息的可能性增加8倍，并且明确的隐私指令虽然减少但并未消除这一效应，即使有保护措施，泄露率仍高于37.8%。我们的研究结果表明，静态基于聊天的安全基准系统性低估了代理部署中的风险，单靠社交背景就足以引发敏感信息的披露，而单轮评估永远无法揭示这些信息。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the inadequacy of existing LLM safety evaluations, which typically test models in isolation, failing to account for the social dynamics present in multi-agent systems. Previous methods have not effectively captured the risks associated with privacy violations in these environments, particularly under social pressure. The proposed Moltbook-style simulation platform allows for the interaction of thousands of LLM agents over a simulated month, revealing that multi-turn evaluations significantly increase privacy violations and that such disclosures can be socially contagious. The paper contributes to understanding privacy risks in AI deployments by demonstrating that static safety benchmarks underestimate these risks, with findings indicating that even with explicit privacy instructions, leakage rates remain high. The methodology involves simulating agent interactions to evaluate privacy outcomes, achieving a privacy violation rate of 45.30% in multi-turn scenarios, which underscores the need for more comprehensive safety evaluations in agentic contexts.

Evolving and Detecting Multi-Turn Deception using Geometric Signatures
Authors: Surender Suresh Kumar, Mary L. Cummings
First: 2026-05-26T20:48:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-26T20:48:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety defenses for large language models (LLMs) are typically trained and evaluated on single-turn prompts, yet real attacks often unfold as indirect, multi-turn probing. To defend against this more nuanced form of deception, we present a unified pipeline that generates realistic multi-turn deceptive question sets via multi-objective genetic prompt optimization with co-evolving mutation operators. We validate this dataset through a human study, which also revealed that early generations yielded the most convincing deception and practical constraints such as adherence filtering and ordering effects. Using this data, we were able to detect deceptive attempts to access prohibited information using simple, explainable geometric signals in embedding space coupled with a lightweight feed-forward classifier. Three geometric features (angular coverage, distance ratio, and linearity) augmented with pairwise similarity statistics led to a compact predictive model that achieved consistently high recall (0.89) across base, reworded, and truncated (three-turn) scenarios, with test-time F1 ranging from 0.74-0.86. The results support a central hypothesis that multi-turn deceptive intent leaves a stable geometric footprint that enables lightweight, transparent screening without expensive end-to-end training. We further discuss responsible uses, limitations, and paths toward larger, more diverse human-evaluated datasets. The primary contribution to artificial intelligence is the multi-objective evolutionary framework for prompt generation, and the engineering application is the deployment of a lightweight geometric detection system for LLM safety infrastructure.
中文标题/摘要
标题：使用几何特征演变和检测多轮欺骗
大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全防御通常在单轮提示上进行训练和评估，但真实攻击往往以间接的多轮探测形式展开。为了防御这种更微妙的欺骗形式，我们提出了一个统一的流程，通过多目标遗传提示优化与共同演变的变异操作生成现实的多轮欺骗问题集。我们通过一项人类研究验证了该数据集，该研究还揭示了早期生成的欺骗最具说服力，以及遵循过滤和排序效应等实际限制。利用这些数据，我们能够使用简单、可解释的几何信号在嵌入空间中检测试图访问禁止信息的欺骗尝试，并结合轻量级前馈分类器。三个几何特征（角度覆盖、距离比和线性）与成对相似性统计相结合，形成了一个紧凑的预测模型，在基础、改写和截断（三轮）场景中实现了一致的高召回率（0.89），测试时F1值范围为0.74-0.86。结果支持一个核心假设，即多轮欺骗意图留下稳定的几何足迹，使得无需昂贵的端到端训练即可实现轻量、透明的筛选。我们进一步讨论了负责任的使用、局限性以及朝向更大、更具多样性的人类评估数据集的路径。对人工智能的主要贡献是用于提示生成的多目标进化框架，工程应用是为LLM安全基础设施部署轻量级几何检测系统。

This research addresses the inadequacy of existing safety defenses for large language models (LLMs), which are typically evaluated on single-turn prompts despite real attacks often occurring in multi-turn interactions. Previous methods have struggled to effectively detect nuanced multi-turn deception, leading to the development of a novel approach that utilizes multi-objective genetic prompt optimization to generate realistic multi-turn deceptive question sets. The proposed method not only enhances the generation of deceptive prompts but also employs a lightweight geometric detection system that identifies deceptive attempts through geometric features in embedding space. The methodology includes a human study to validate the generated dataset and a predictive model that achieved high recall (0.89) and F1 scores ranging from 0.74 to 0.86 across various scenarios, demonstrating the effectiveness of the approach in detecting multi-turn deception and supporting its goals of improving LLM safety infrastructure.

$D^2$-Monitor: Dynamic Safety Monitoring for Diffusion LLMs via Hesitation-Aware Routing
Authors: Aoxi Liu, Yupeng Chen, James Oldfield, Guanzhe Hong, Junchi Yu, Baoyuan Wu, Philip Torr, Adel Bibi
First: 2026-05-25T14:22:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-25T14:22:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite the emergence of diffusion large language models (D-LLMs) as an alternative to autoregressive large language models (AR-LLMs), safety monitoring for D-LLMs remains largely unexplored. Unlike AR-LLMs, D-LLMs generate text through a multi-step denoising process, exposing intermediate hidden representations that may contain safety-relevant information unavailable in standard single-step monitoring setups. Motivated by the suitability of lightweight probes for always-on monitoring, we analyze which trajectory-level signals best indicate when such probes are likely to struggle. We find that the most informative signal is safety hesitation: intermediate hidden states repeatedly falling within a small margin of the probe's decision boundary. The number of such hesitation steps in D-LLM's trajectory predicts probe failure effectively, providing a proxy of sample difficulty. Building on this analysis, we propose $D^2$-Monitor, a bi-level safety monitor for D-LLMs. $D^2$-Monitor adopts a lightweight probe as an always-on monitor to jointly estimate hesitation and perform base classification. When the hesitation level exceeds a threshold, a more expressive but computationally heavier probe is activated. This dynamic routing mechanism allocates monitoring resources efficiently at test time. Evaluated on 3 datasets (WildguardMix, ToxicChat, OpenAI-Moderation) across 4 D-LLMs, $D^2$-Monitor achieves state-of-the-art performance with a compact parameter footprint ($\leq$ 0.85M parameters), and exhibits the best trade-off between effectiveness and efficiency relative to 8 baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：$D^2$-监控器：通过考虑犹豫的动态安全监控扩散大语言模型
尽管扩散大语言模型（D-LLMs）作为自回归大语言模型（AR-LLMs）的替代方案已出现，但对D-LLMs的安全监控仍然基本未被探索。与AR-LLMs不同，D-LLMs通过多步骤去噪过程生成文本，暴露出可能包含安全相关信息的中间隐藏表示，而这些信息在标准单步监控设置中不可用。基于轻量级探针适合于始终在线监控的动机，我们分析了哪些轨迹级信号最能指示这些探针可能遇到困难。我们发现，最具信息量的信号是安全犹豫：中间隐藏状态反复落在探针决策边界的小范围内。D-LLM轨迹中的这种犹豫步骤数量有效预测探针失败，提供了样本难度的代理。基于此分析，我们提出了$D^2$-监控器，这是一个针对D-LLMs的双层安全监控器。$D^2$-监控器采用轻量级探针作为始终在线监控器，联合估计犹豫并进行基础分类。当犹豫水平超过阈值时，将激活一个更具表现力但计算负担更重的探针。该动态路由机制在测试时有效分配监控资源。在3个数据集（WildguardMix、ToxicChat、OpenAI-Moderation）上评估4个D-LLMs，$D^2$-监控器以紧凑的参数占用（≤ 0.85M参数）实现了最先进的性能，并在相对于8个基线之间展现了最佳的有效性与效率的权衡。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the gap in safety monitoring for diffusion large language models (D-LLMs), which generate text through a multi-step denoising process, unlike autoregressive models. Previous methods have not effectively utilized the intermediate hidden representations of D-LLMs, leading to insufficient safety monitoring. The proposed approach, $D^2$-Monitor, introduces a bi-level safety monitoring system that leverages lightweight probes to detect safety hesitation in the model's output, activating a more complex probe only when necessary. This method is well-motivated as it aims to optimize resource allocation during monitoring. The contribution of the paper lies in its innovative dynamic routing mechanism, which enhances monitoring efficiency while maintaining high performance. Evaluated on three datasets, $D^2$-Monitor achieves state-of-the-art results with a compact parameter footprint, demonstrating a superior balance between effectiveness and efficiency compared to eight baseline methods.

Reflect-Guard: Enhancing LLM Safeguards against Adversarial Prompts via Logical Self-Reflection
Authors: Lixing Lin, Juli You, Yue Li, Luyun Lin, Yiqing Wang, Zhen Zhang, Moxuan Zheng
First: 2026-05-24T02:58:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-24T02:58:21+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 2 figures, and 4 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) safety classifiers such as Llama Guard are effective at detecting overtly harmful prompts but remain vulnerable to adversarial jailbreak attacks that disguise malicious intent through role-play scenarios, fictional framing, and indirect requests. We present Reflect-Guard, a method that augments LLM-based safety classifiers with chain-of-thought self-reflection capabilities through parameter-efficient fine-tuning. Our approach distills analytical reasoning from GPT-4o-mini into structured reflection annotations, then trains Llama-Guard-3-8B via QLoRA to generate logical self-reflections before issuing safety verdicts. Using only 1000 training examples and updating just 0.5% of model parameters (~42M), Reflect-Guard achieves substantial improvements on two challenging benchmarks. On WildGuardTest, F1 score improves from 0.770 to 0.842 (+7.2 pp), with recall on adversarial prompts increasing from 0.513 to 0.921 (+40.8 pp). On JailbreakBench, the attack success rate drops from 10.3% to 1.8%, representing an 82.5% relative reduction. These gains are especially pronounced on adversarial inputs, where the explicit reasoning step enables the model to see through obfuscation techniques that defeat standard pattern-matching approaches. Our results demonstrate that teaching safety classifiers to reason about adversarial intent, rather than simply classify surface patterns, is a promising direction for robust LLM safety.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Reflect-Guard：通过逻辑自我反思增强大型语言模型对抗性提示的安全防护
大型语言模型（LLM）安全分类器如Llama Guard在检测明显有害提示方面有效，但仍然容易受到通过角色扮演场景、虚构框架和间接请求伪装恶意意图的对抗性越狱攻击的影响。我们提出了Reflect-Guard，这是一种通过参数高效微调增强LLM基础安全分类器的链式思维自我反思能力的方法。我们的方法从GPT-4o-mini中提炼分析推理，形成结构化反思注释，然后通过QLoRA训练Llama-Guard-3-8B，以在发出安全裁决之前生成逻辑自我反思。仅使用1000个训练样本并更新0.5%的模型参数（约4200万），Reflect-Guard在两个具有挑战性的基准测试中取得了显著改善。在WildGuardTest中，F1分数从0.770提高到0.842（+7.2个百分点），对抗性提示的召回率从0.513提高到0.921（+40.8个百分点）。在JailbreakBench中，攻击成功率从10.3%降至1.8%，相对减少82.5%。这些提升在对抗性输入上尤为明显，明确的推理步骤使模型能够看穿击败标准模式匹配方法的混淆技术。我们的结果表明，教导安全分类器推理对抗性意图，而不仅仅是分类表面模式，是增强LLM安全性的一个有前景的方向。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the limitations of existing large language model (LLM) safety classifiers, which effectively detect harmful prompts but are susceptible to adversarial jailbreak attacks that mask malicious intent. Previous methods primarily relied on surface pattern recognition, which failed to counteract sophisticated obfuscation techniques. The proposed Reflect-Guard method enhances LLM safety classifiers by incorporating chain-of-thought self-reflection capabilities through parameter-efficient fine-tuning, allowing the model to reason about adversarial intent. This approach is well-motivated as it shifts the focus from mere classification to analytical reasoning. The methodology involves distilling reasoning from GPT-4o-mini into structured annotations and training Llama-Guard-3-8B with QLoRA on a limited dataset. The results show significant performance improvements on two benchmarks, with the F1 score on WildGuardTest increasing from 0.770 to 0.842 and the attack success rate on JailbreakBench dropping from 10.3% to 1.8%, demonstrating the effectiveness of the proposed method in enhancing LLM safety against adversarial prompts.
本研究解决了现有大型语言模型（LLM）安全分类器的局限性，这些分类器对明显有害的提示有效，但容易受到使用欺骗性框架的对抗性越狱攻击的影响。以往的方法主要依赖于模式匹配，未能检测到细微的威胁，而提出的Reflect-Guard通过引入链式思维自我反思来增强安全分类器，采用参数高效的微调方法。该方法将GPT-4o-mini的推理提炼为结构化注释，并训练Llama-Guard-3-8B在做出安全评估之前生成逻辑自我反思。该方法在WildGuardTest等基准测试中显示出显著改善，F1分数从0.770提高到0.842，在JailbreakBench中攻击成功率从10.3%降至1.8%。这些结果表明，赋予安全分类器推理能力显著增强了其识别对抗性提示的能力，支持了更强大LLM安全性的目标。
RouteScan: A Non-Intrusive Approach to Auditing MoE LLMs Safety via Expert Routing Telemetry
Authors: Bo Lv, Zhiheng Xu, KeDong Xiu, Ruyi Ding, Tianhang Zheng, Zhibo Wang, Kui Ren
First: 2026-05-24T02:06:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-24T02:06:44+00:00
Comments: 20 pages. Under submission
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures have become an increasingly important paradigm for scaling Large Language Models (LLMs). As MoE models are increasingly deployed in real-world services, safety auditing becomes necessary to verify whether these models produce or facilitate harmful behaviors during operation. However, existing content-based auditing methods typically require access to user prompts, model inputs, or generated outputs, potentially exposing sensitive user information and creating a fundamental tension between LLM safety and user privacy. On the other hand, we observe that, in MoE models, sparse expert routing maps different inputs to activate different expert-execution patterns, producing measurable footprints in low-level GPU execution telemetry. Inspired by this observation, we propose RouteScan, a non-intrusive auditing framework for detecting harmful behaviors through GPU-level expert routing telemetry. Specifically, RouteScan utilizes the number of active GPU threads allocated to expert modules during the prefilling phase as a discriminative micro-architectural fingerprint, and builds a lightweight detection pipeline that isolates cross-domain invariant risk indicators for the precise identification of malicious prompts. Comprehensive evaluations on open-source MoE LLMs with distinct routing designs demonstrate that RouteScan achieves strong generalization, with an AUROC exceeding 0.93 on unseen harmful domains and 0.96 under novel jailbreak wrappers. Moreover, empirical inversion tests show that the collected expert routing telemetry provides limited information for prompt reconstruction, suggesting a practical privacy advantage over content-based auditing methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RouteScan：通过专家路由遥测对MoE LLMs安全性进行非侵入式审计的方法
混合专家（MoE）架构已成为扩展大型语言模型（LLMs）日益重要的范式。随着MoE模型在现实服务中的逐步部署，安全审计变得必要，以验证这些模型在操作过程中是否产生或促进有害行为。然而，现有的基于内容的审计方法通常需要访问用户提示、模型输入或生成的输出，这可能暴露敏感用户信息，并在LLM安全性与用户隐私之间产生根本性矛盾。另一方面，我们观察到，在MoE模型中，稀疏的专家路由将不同的输入映射到激活不同的专家执行模式，产生可测量的低级GPU执行遥测足迹。受此观察启发，我们提出了RouteScan，一个通过GPU级专家路由遥测检测有害行为的非侵入式审计框架。具体而言，RouteScan利用在预填充阶段分配给专家模块的活跃GPU线程数量作为区分性的微架构指纹，并构建一个轻量级检测管道，隔离跨域不变风险指标，以精确识别恶意提示。对具有不同路由设计的开源MoE LLMs的全面评估表明，RouteScan实现了强大的泛化能力，在未见的有害领域上AUROC超过0.93，在新型越狱包装下达到0.96。此外，经验反演测试表明，收集的专家路由遥测提供的提示重构信息有限，表明相较于基于内容的审计方法具有实际的隐私优势。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the growing need for safety auditing in Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures used in Large Language Models (LLMs), which are increasingly deployed in real-world applications. Traditional content-based auditing methods pose privacy risks by requiring access to sensitive user data, creating a conflict between ensuring model safety and protecting user privacy. The proposed approach, RouteScan, differs by utilizing GPU-level expert routing telemetry to audit model behavior without accessing user prompts or outputs, thus maintaining privacy while effectively identifying harmful behaviors. The paper contributes a non-intrusive framework that leverages active GPU thread counts during the model's execution to create a detection pipeline for malicious prompts. Evaluations on various open-source MoE LLMs show that RouteScan achieves high performance, with an AUROC of over 0.93 on unseen harmful domains, indicating its effectiveness in supporting safety auditing goals while preserving user privacy.
本研究解决了在大型语言模型（LLM）中使用的混合专家（MoE）架构中日益增长的安全审计需求，因为现有的基于内容的方法存在泄露敏感用户信息的风险。传统的审计方法需要访问用户提示或模型输出，这可能会危及隐私。相比之下，所提出的RouteScan框架利用GPU级专家路由遥测，捕捉不同专家的执行模式，而无需直接访问用户数据。该方法的动机在于观察到这些路由模式会产生可测量的足迹，可用于检测有害行为。本文的贡献在于其能够以高精度识别恶意提示，在未见过的有害领域上实现超过0.93的AUROC，在新型越狱包装下达到0.96，同时通过限制可用于提示重构的信息来维护用户隐私。
BarrierSteer: LLM Safety via Learning Barrier Steering
Authors: Thanh Q. Tran, Arun Verma, Kiwan Wong, Bryan Kian Hsiang Low, Daniela Rus, Wei Xiao
First: 2026-02-23T18:19:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-21T18:01:19+00:00
Comments: This paper introduces SafeBarrier, a framework that enforces safety in large language models by steering their latent representations with control barrier functions during inference, reducing adversarial and unsafe outputs
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Despite the strong performance of large language models (LLMs) across diverse tasks, their susceptibility to adversarial attacks and unsafe content generation remains a significant obstacle to deployment, particularly in high-stakes settings. Addressing this challenge requires safety mechanisms that are both practically effective and theoretically grounded. In this paper, we introduce BarrierSteer, a novel inference-time framework that improves response safety by embedding learned nonlinear safety constraints directly into the model's latent representation space. BarrierSteer treats hidden-state safety classifiers as Control Barrier Functions (CBFs), enabling constraint-guided steering of unsafe latent trajectories during generation. By composing multiple safety constraints through efficient constraint merging without modifying the underlying LLM parameters, BarrierSteer preserves model utility. We provide theoretical results showing that applying CBFs in the latent space yields a principled, modular, and computationally efficient approach for steering with respect to learned safety constraints, with guarantees conditional on the learned barriers capturing the intended safety property. Our extensive experimental results across multiple model families and datasets demonstrate that BarrierSteer substantially reduces adversarial attack success rates and unsafe generations, outperforming the existing method. The code is available in our \href{https://github.com/thanhquangtran/BarrierSteer}{GitHub repository}.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BarrierSteer：通过学习障碍引导实现LLM安全
尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）在各种任务中表现出色，但它们对对抗性攻击和不安全内容生成的易感性仍然是部署中的一个重大障碍，特别是在高风险环境中。解决这一挑战需要既有效又有理论基础的安全机制。本文介绍了BarrierSteer，这是一种新颖的推理时框架，通过将学习到的非线性安全约束直接嵌入模型的潜在表示空间来提高响应安全性。BarrierSteer将隐藏状态安全分类器视为控制障碍函数（CBFs），使得在生成过程中能够对不安全的潜在轨迹进行约束引导。通过高效的约束合并组合多个安全约束，而不修改底层LLM参数，BarrierSteer保持了模型的实用性。我们提供了理论结果，表明在潜在空间中应用CBFs提供了一种原则性、模块化和计算高效的引导方法，能够根据学习到的障碍捕捉预期的安全属性。我们在多个模型系列和数据集上的广泛实验结果表明，BarrierSteer显著降低了对抗性攻击成功率和不安全生成，优于现有方法。代码可在我们的\href{https://github.com/thanhquangtran/BarrierSteer}{GitHub仓库}中获取。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the critical issue of safety in large language models (LLMs), which are prone to adversarial attacks and unsafe content generation, particularly in sensitive applications. Previous methods lacked effective safety mechanisms that were both practical and theoretically sound, leading to vulnerabilities during model deployment. The proposed approach, BarrierSteer, introduces a novel framework that integrates learned nonlinear safety constraints into the model's latent representation space, utilizing Control Barrier Functions (CBFs) to guide the generation process without altering the LLM parameters. This method is well-motivated as it aims to enhance safety while maintaining model utility. The paper contributes a principled and computationally efficient strategy for steering LLMs in accordance with safety constraints, demonstrating through extensive experiments that BarrierSteer significantly reduces the rates of adversarial attacks and unsafe outputs compared to existing methods, thus supporting its safety goals effectively.

Revisiting Robustness for LLM Safety Alignment via Selective Geometry Control
Authors: Yonghui Yang, Wenjian Tao, Jilong Liu, Xingyu Zhu, Junfeng Fang, Weibiao Huang, Le Wu, Richang Hong, Tat-Sent Chua
First: 2026-02-07T03:46:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-21T07:39:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Safety alignment of large language models remains brittle under domain shift and noisy preference supervision. Most existing robust alignment methods focus on uncertainty in alignment data, while overlooking optimization-induced fragility in preference-based objectives. In this work, we revisit robustness for LLM safety alignment from an optimization geometry perspective, and argue that robustness failures cannot be addressed by data-centric methods alone. We propose \textit{ShaPO}, a geometry-aware preference optimization framework that enforces worst-case alignment objectives via selective geometry control over alignment-critical parameter subspace. By avoiding uniform geometry constraints, ShaPO mitigates the over-regularization that can harm robustness under distribution shift. We instantiate ShaPO at two levels: token-level ShaPO stabilizes likelihood-based surrogate optimization, while reward-level ShaPO enforces reward-consistent optimization under noisy supervision. Across diverse safety benchmarks and noisy preference settings, ShaPO consistently improves safety robustness over popular preference optimization methods. Moreover, ShaPO composes cleanly with data-robust objectives, yielding additional gains and empirically supporting the proposed optimization-geometry perspective. The code is available at https://github.com/liujilong0116/ShaPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过选择性几何控制重新审视大型语言模型的安全对齐鲁棒性
大型语言模型的安全对齐在领域转移和噪声偏好监督下仍然脆弱。现有的大多数鲁棒对齐方法关注对齐数据的不确定性，而忽视了偏好目标中由优化引起的脆弱性。在本研究中，我们从优化几何的角度重新审视LLM安全对齐的鲁棒性，并认为鲁棒性失败不能仅通过以数据为中心的方法来解决。我们提出了\textit{ShaPO}，一种几何感知的偏好优化框架，通过对对齐关键参数子空间的选择性几何控制来强制执行最坏情况对齐目标。通过避免均匀几何约束，ShaPO减轻了在分布转移下可能损害鲁棒性的过度正则化。我们在两个层面上实例化ShaPO：令牌级ShaPO稳定基于似然的替代优化，而奖励级ShaPO在噪声监督下强制执行奖励一致的优化。在多样的安全基准和噪声偏好设置中，ShaPO始终优于流行的偏好优化方法，提高了安全鲁棒性。此外，ShaPO与数据鲁棒目标良好组合，带来额外收益，并在经验上支持所提出的优化几何视角。代码可在https://github.com/liujilong0116/ShaPO获取。

The research addresses the challenges of safety alignment in large language models (LLMs), particularly their vulnerability to domain shifts and noisy preference supervision. This approach is well-motivated as it enhances robustness against distribution shifts. On-Policy Consistency Training Improves LLM Safety with Minimal Capability Degradation
Authors: Andy Han, Kristina Fujimoto, Avidan Shah, Kiet Nguyen, Kai Xu, Chen Yueh-Han, Ilia Sucholutsky, Rico Angell
First: 2026-05-20T23:56:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-20T23:56:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Aligned models can misbehave in several ways: they are often sycophantic, fall victim to jailbreaks, or fail to include appropriate safety warnings. Consistency training is a promising new alignment paradigm to mitigate such failures by training invariants into the model using contrastive input pairs. Existing consistency training procedures generate the supervision signal once, offline, and use supervised fine-tuning (SFT) to update the model. Unfortunately, the resulting models tend to merely memorize the surface forms of the training distribution and thus generalize poorly and regress in their capabilities. We introduce On-Policy Consistency Training (OPCT), a new consistency training approach where the objective is computed over the model's own responses to prompts, supervised by itself conditioned on corresponding contrastive prompts. We evaluate OPCT on three safety axes: sycophancy, jailbreaking, and safety awareness. Across three model families, OPCT outperforms its SFT counterpart on all safety desiderata. It nearly halves the sycophancy rate relative to baseline (8.1% vs. 15.4%, compared to 11.2% for SFT). Under an adaptive per-target attacker, OPCT holds jailbreak defense success near 99% on held-out jailbreak behaviors, whereas SFT achieves 87% on average. On safety awareness, OPCT outperforms SFT in two out of three models, and matches it on the other. OPCT also largely avoids the capability regressions that SFT induces, such as a 28-point drop on MATH-500. Our results suggest that consistency training is best implemented as OPCT rather than as SFT, especially when generalization beyond the training distribution is desired.

标题：基于策略的一致性训练通过最小能力退化提高大型语言模型的安全性
对齐模型可能以多种方式表现不当：它们往往表现得过于谄媚，容易受到越狱攻击，或未能包含适当的安全警告。一致性训练是一种有前景的新对齐范式，通过使用对比输入对将不变性训练到模型中，以减轻这些失败。现有的一致性训练程序仅在离线状态下生成一次监督信号，并使用监督微调（SFT）来更新模型。不幸的是，结果模型往往仅仅记忆训练分布的表面形式，因此泛化能力差，能力退化。我们引入了基于策略的一致性训练（OPCT），这是一种新的一致性训练方法，其目标是基于模型对提示的自身响应进行计算，由相应的对比提示进行自我监督。我们在三个安全维度上评估OPCT：谄媚、越狱和安全意识。在三种模型系列中，OPCT在所有安全要求上均优于其SFT对应物。与基线相比，谄媚率几乎减半（8.1%对15.4%，而SFT为11.2%）。在适应性每个目标攻击者下，OPCT在保留的越狱行为上保持近99%的越狱防御成功率，而SFT平均为87%。在安全意识方面，OPCT在三种模型中的两种上优于SFT，另一种则持平。OPCT还在很大程度上避免了SFT引起的能力退化，例如在MATH-500上下降28分。我们的结果表明，一致性训练最好以OPCT的形式实施，而不是SFT，特别是在希望超越训练分布进行泛化时。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the shortcomings of aligned models that often exhibit undesirable behaviors such as sycophancy and vulnerability to jailbreaks. Traditional consistency training methods generate supervision signals offline and rely on supervised fine-tuning (SFT), leading to poor generalization and capability regression. The proposed On-Policy Consistency Training (OPCT) method improves upon these existing approaches by computing objectives based on the model's own responses to prompts, thereby enhancing self-supervision. This paper contributes to the field by demonstrating that OPCT significantly reduces sycophancy rates and improves jailbreak defense while maintaining model capabilities, outperforming SFT across multiple safety metrics. The methodology was evaluated on three model families, showing that OPCT nearly halves the sycophancy rate and achieves a 99% success rate in jailbreak defense, while also avoiding the capability regressions seen with SFT, indicating its effectiveness in promoting model safety without sacrificing performance.

CR4T: Rewrite-Based Guardrails for Adolescent LLM Safety
Authors: Heajun An, Qi Zhang, Vedanth Achanta, Jin-Hee Cho
First: 2026-05-20T18:16:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-20T18:16:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly embedded in adolescent digital environments, mediating information seeking, advice, and emotionally sensitive interactions. Yet existing safety mechanisms remain largely grounded in adult-centric norms and operationalize safety through refusal-oriented suppression. While such approaches may reduce immediate policy violations, they can also create conversational dead-ends, limit constructive guidance, and fail to address the developmental vulnerabilities inherent in adolescent-AI interactions. We argue that adolescent LLM safety should be framed not solely as a filtering problem, but as a socio-technical, developmentally aligned transformation problem. To operationalize this perspective, we propose Critique-and-Revise-for-Teenagers (CR4T), a model-agnostic safeguarding framework that selectively reconstructs unsafe or refusal-style outputs into ageappropriate, guidance-oriented responses while preserving benign intent. CR4T combines lightweight risk detection with domain-conditioned rewriting to remove risk-amplifying content, reduce unnecessary conversational shutdown, and introduce developmentally appropriate guidance. Experimental results show that targeted rewriting substantially reduces unsafe and refusal-oriented outcomes while avoiding unnecessary intervention on acceptable interactions. These findings suggest that selective response reconstruction offers a more human-centered alternative to refusal-centric guardrails for adolescent-facing LLM systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CR4T：基于重写的青少年大型语言模型安全防护
大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地嵌入青少年的数字环境中，调解信息搜索、建议和情感敏感的互动。然而，现有的安全机制仍然主要基于成人中心的规范，并通过拒绝导向的压制来实现安全。虽然这种方法可能减少即时的政策违规，但也可能造成对话的死胡同，限制建设性指导，并未能解决青少年与人工智能互动中固有的发展脆弱性。我们认为，青少年LLM安全不应仅仅被视为过滤问题，而应被视为一个社会技术、发展对齐的转型问题。为了实现这一视角，我们提出了针对青少年的批评与修订（CR4T），这是一个模型无关的安全框架，选择性地将不安全或拒绝风格的输出重构为适龄的、指导导向的响应，同时保持良好的意图。CR4T结合轻量级风险检测与领域条件重写，以去除风险放大内容，减少不必要的对话中断，并引入发展适宜的指导。实验结果表明，针对性重写显著减少了不安全和拒绝导向的结果，同时避免了对可接受互动的不必要干预。这些发现表明，选择性响应重构为面向青少年的LLM系统提供了一种更以人为本的替代方案，取代了以拒绝为中心的防护措施。

The proposed approach, Critique-and-Revise-for-Teenagers (CR4T), shifts the focus from mere filtering to a socio-technical transformation that reconstructs unsafe outputs into age-appropriate, guidance-oriented responses, thus addressing the limitations of prior methods. The paper contributes a model-agnostic framework that integrates risk detection with domain-specific rewriting, demonstrating through experiments that this targeted rewriting significantly reduces unsafe and refusal-oriented outcomes while maintaining acceptable interactions. The results indicate that CR4T provides a more human-centered alternative for ensuring safety in adolescent LLM applications.

Adaptive Probe-based Steering for Robust LLM Jailbreaking
Authors: Junxi Chen, Junhao Dong, Xiaohua Xie
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-05-19T06:11:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-19T06:11:04+00:00
Comments: 19 pages, 13 figures, accepted by ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Recent work has demonstrated the potential of contrastive steering for jailbreaking Large Language Models (LLMs). However, existing methods rely on limited and inherently biased contrastive prompts and require laborious manual tuning of steering strength, limiting their robustness and effectiveness. In this paper, we leverage the idea of model extraction to guide the learned steering vectors to approximate the ideal one and propose tuning the steering strength adaptively based on contrastive activations' statistics. Experiments demonstrate that our method notably improves the effectiveness and robustness of probe-based steering, without any extra contrastive prompts or laborious manual tuning. Being an attack paper, this paper focuses on revealing the breakdown of fortified LLMs, raising the average harmfulness score from 6\% to 70\%. Our code is available at https://github.com/fhdnskfbeuv/adaptiveSteering.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于自适应探针的鲁棒LLM越狱引导
最近的研究展示了对比引导在越狱大型语言模型（LLMs）中的潜力。然而，现有方法依赖于有限且固有偏见的对比提示，并需要繁琐的手动调节引导强度，限制了其鲁棒性和有效性。本文利用模型提取的思想，引导学习到的引导向量逼近理想向量，并提出基于对比激活统计自适应调节引导强度。实验表明，我们的方法显著提高了基于探针的引导的有效性和鲁棒性，无需额外的对比提示或繁琐的手动调节。作为一篇攻击论文，本文重点揭示了强化LLMs的崩溃，将平均危害评分从6\%提高到70\%。我们的代码可在https://github.com/fhdnskfbeuv/adaptiveSteering获取。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the limitations of existing contrastive steering methods for jailbreaking Large Language Models (LLMs), which often rely on biased prompts and require extensive manual tuning, thus compromising their robustness. The proposed approach introduces adaptive tuning of steering strength based on the statistical analysis of contrastive activations, which enhances the effectiveness and robustness of the steering process without the need for additional prompts or manual adjustments. The contribution of this paper lies in its novel method that significantly increases the average harmfulness score of LLMs from 6% to 70%, demonstrating its potential to effectively expose vulnerabilities in fortified models. The methodology involves leveraging model extraction to guide steering vectors, ultimately achieving a more reliable and efficient jailbreaking technique.

LLM-Safety Evaluations Lack Robustness
Authors: Tim Beyer, Sophie Xhonneux, Simon Geisler, Gauthier Gidel, Leo Schwinn, Stephan Günnemann
First: 2025-03-04T12:55:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-18T17:54:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this paper, we argue that current safety alignment research efforts for large language models are hindered by many intertwined sources of noise, such as small datasets, methodological inconsistencies, and unreliable evaluation setups. This can, at times, make it impossible to evaluate and compare attacks and defenses fairly, thereby slowing progress. We systematically analyze the LLM safety evaluation pipeline, covering dataset curation, optimization strategies for automated red-teaming, response generation, and response evaluation using LLM judges. At each stage, we identify key issues and highlight their practical impact. We also propose a set of guidelines for reducing noise and bias in evaluations of future attack and defense papers. Lastly, we offer an opposing perspective, highlighting practical reasons for existing limitations. We believe that addressing the outlined problems in future research will improve the field's ability to generate easily comparable results and make measurable progress.

Babel: Jailbreaking Safety Attention via Obfuscation Distribution Optimized Sampling
Authors: Ziwei Wang, Jing Chen, Ruichao Liang, Zhi Wang, Yebo Feng, Ju Jia, Ruiying Du, Cong Wu, Yang Liu
First: 2026-05-18T07:27:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-18T07:27:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite rigorous safety alignment, Large Language Models (LLMs) remain vulnerable to jailbreak attacks. Existing black-box methods often rely on heuristic templates or exhaustive trials, lacking mechanistic interpretability and query efficiency. In this study, we investigate an intrinsic vulnerability in the safety mechanisms of LLMs, where safety alignment relies on a small set of sparsely distributed attention heads, leaving much of the representational space weakly monitored. We formalize this phenomenon with a mathematical jailbreaking model that characterizes the delicate boundary of effective text obfuscation and analytically explains observed jailbreak behaviors. Guided by this model, we propose Babel, an efficient black-box attack framework that exploits the identified safety gap through systematic obfuscation sampling with iterative, feedback-driven distribution refinement, enabling reliable and high-success jailbreak attacks without access to model internals. Comprehensive evaluations on frontier commercial models demonstrate that Babel achieves state-of-the-art attack success rates and superior query efficiency. Specifically, compared to state-of-the-art methods, Babel increases the attack success rate on GPT-4o from 41.33% to 82.67% and on Claude-3-5-haiku from 38.33% to 78.33% within an average of 40 queries, providing a robust red-teaming methodology for LLMs safety research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：巴别：通过模糊分布优化采样破解安全注意力
尽管进行了严格的安全对齐，大型语言模型（LLMs）仍然容易受到越狱攻击。现有的黑箱方法通常依赖于启发式模板或穷举试验，缺乏机制可解释性和查询效率。在本研究中，我们调查了LLMs安全机制中的内在脆弱性，其中安全对齐依赖于一小组稀疏分布的注意力头，导致大部分表示空间监控不足。我们用数学越狱模型形式化这一现象，描述有效文本模糊化的微妙边界，并分析观察到的越狱行为。在该模型的指导下，我们提出了Babel，一个高效的黑箱攻击框架，通过系统的模糊采样和迭代反馈驱动的分布优化，利用识别出的安全漏洞，实现可靠且高成功率的越狱攻击，而无需访问模型内部。对前沿商业模型的全面评估表明，Babel实现了最先进的攻击成功率和优越的查询效率。具体而言，与最先进的方法相比，Babel将GPT-4o的攻击成功率从41.33%提高到82.67%，将Claude-3-5-haiku的攻击成功率从38.33%提高到78.33%，平均在40个查询内，提供了一种强大的红队方法论用于LLMs安全研究。

IndicSafe: A Benchmark for Evaluating Multilingual LLM Safety in South Asia
Authors: Priyaranjan Pattnayak, Sanchari Chowdhuri
First: 2026-03-18T16:54:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-15T17:06:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As large language models (LLMs) are deployed in multilingual settings, their safety behavior in culturally diverse, low-resource languages remains poorly understood. We present the first systematic evaluation of LLM safety across 12 Indic languages, spoken by over 1.2 billion people but underrepresented in LLM training data. Using a dataset of 6,000 culturally grounded prompts spanning caste, religion, gender, health, and politics, we assess 10 leading LLMs on translated variants of the prompt. Our analysis reveals significant safety drift: cross-language agreement is just 12.8\%, and \texttt{SAFE} rate variance exceeds 17\% across languages. Some models over-refuse benign prompts in low-resource scripts, overflag politically sensitive topics, while others fail to flag unsafe generations. We quantify these failures using prompt-level entropy, category bias scores, and multilingual consistency indices. Our findings highlight critical safety generalization gaps in multilingual LLMs and show that safety alignment does not transfer evenly across languages. We release \textsc{IndicSafe}, the first benchmark to enable culturally informed safety evaluation for Indic deployments, and advocate for language-aware alignment strategies grounded in regional harms.

Graph-Regularized Sparse Autoencoders for LLM Safety Steering
Authors: Jehyeok Yeon, Federico Cinus, Yifan Wu, Luca Luceri
First: 2025-12-07T04:46:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-15T09:56:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) are increasingly used to extract activation directions for inference-time steering, but their standard sparsity objective treats latent features as independent. This prior can be poorly matched to high-level safety behaviors, where refusal and harmful compliance appear to depend on distributed structure in activation space. We introduce Graph-Regularized Sparse Autoencoders (GSAE), a dictionary-learning method that learns safety-steering directions by smoothing SAE decoder vectors over a neuron co-activation graph and applying the resulting direction bank through a two-gate runtime controller. Empirically, GSAE improves selective refusal across JailbreakBench, HarmBench, and XSTest, increasing harmful-request refusal while keeping benign-prompt refusals low. On Llama-3-8B, replacing the standard SAE with GSAE in an otherwise identical pipeline improves $Δ_s$ by $20.1$ points on JailbreakBench and $16.8$ points on HarmBench. GSAE outperforms activation-steering baselines and black-box guardrails, preserves benign-task performance, generalizes across Llama-3, Mistral, Qwen 2.5, and Phi-4, and remains strong under black-box and gray-box jailbreak attacks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：图正则化稀疏自编码器用于大型语言模型安全引导
稀疏自编码器（SAE）越来越多地用于提取推理时引导的激活方向，但其标准稀疏性目标将潜在特征视为独立。这一先验可能与高层次的安全行为不匹配，其中拒绝和有害的顺从似乎依赖于激活空间中的分布结构。我们引入图正则化稀疏自编码器（GSAE），这是一种字典学习方法，通过在神经元共同激活图上平滑SAE解码器向量来学习安全引导方向，并通过双门运行时控制器应用结果方向库。实证结果表明，GSAE在JailbreakBench、HarmBench和XSTest上改善了选择性拒绝，增加了有害请求的拒绝，同时保持良性提示的拒绝率较低。在Llama-3-8B上，在其他条件相同的管道中用GSAE替换标准SAE，使得JailbreakBench上的$Δ_s$提高了$20.1$点，HarmBench上提高了$16.8$点。GSAE优于激活引导基线和黑箱护栏，保持良性任务性能，在Llama-3、Mistral、Qwen 2.5和Phi-4上具有良好的泛化能力，并在黑箱和灰箱越狱攻击下表现强劲。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the limitations of standard sparse autoencoders (SAEs) in safety steering for large language models (LLMs), where the independence assumption of latent features fails to capture the distributed nature of safety behaviors. Previous methods inadequately handle the interdependencies in activation space, leading to suboptimal performance in refusal and compliance tasks. The proposed Graph-Regularized Sparse Autoencoders (GSAE) improve upon these methods by incorporating a neuron co-activation graph to smooth decoder vectors, enhancing the learning of safety-steering directions. This approach is well-motivated as it directly targets the structural dependencies in activation space. The paper demonstrates that GSAE significantly enhances selective refusal performance on tasks such as JailbreakBench and HarmBench, achieving improvements of 20.1 points and 16.8 points, respectively, while maintaining benign-task performance and generalizing across multiple LLM architectures.

Benchmark of Benchmarks: Unpacking Influence and Code Repository Quality in LLM Safety Benchmarks
Authors: Junjie Chu, Xinyue Shen, Ye Leng, Michael Backes, Yun Shen, Yang Zhang
First: 2026-03-03T09:10:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-14T18:30:07+00:00
Comments: 24 pages. 19 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid expansion of research in LLM safety presents challenges in tracking advancements, making benchmarks important evaluation infrastructures for identifying key trends and facilitating systematic comparisons. Yet no systematic assessment exists of their code quality and runnability, nor of what factors are associated with the community's adoption of certain benchmarks over others. To address this gap, we conduct a systematic measurement study of 31 LLM safety benchmarks (covering prompt injection, jailbreak, and hallucination) with 382 non-benchmark papers as a control group, combining automated static analysis, human runnability testing (220+ person-hours), and bibliometric analysis. We find that only 39\% of benchmark repositories can run without modification, only 16\% provide flawless installation guides, and a mere 6\% include ethical considerations despite containing potentially harmful content. These deficiencies persist across the study period with no significant improvement. Analyzing adoption factors, we find that benchmark adoption correlates with author prominence and code runnability, but not with code quality standards such as Pylint score and maintainability, suggesting that the community's benchmark selection does not reward higher coding standards. Based on these results, we identify potential safety and reliability concerns. Some safety benchmark repositories openly expose harmful content, such as successful jailbreak responses, without any ethical warning or access control, effectively serving as unguarded attack resources. Furthermore, when benchmarks require ad-hoc modifications to run, downstream safety evaluations across different papers may not be comparable. We present case studies illustrating these concrete consequences and propose a targeted checklist to help benchmark contributors improve code quality, documentation, and ethical practices.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基准中的基准：解读LLM安全基准中的影响力和代码库质量
LLM安全研究的快速扩展带来了跟踪进展的挑战，使得基准成为识别关键趋势和促进系统比较的重要评估基础设施。然而，目前尚无对其代码质量和可运行性的系统评估，也没有研究社区对某些基准的采用与其他基准之间的关联因素。为了解决这一空白，我们对31个LLM安全基准（涵盖提示注入、越狱和幻觉）进行系统测量研究，并以382篇非基准论文作为对照组，结合自动静态分析、人为可运行性测试（220+人小时）和文献计量分析。我们发现，只有39%的基准代码库可以在不修改的情况下运行，只有16%提供无瑕疵的安装指南，尽管包含潜在有害内容，但仅有6%考虑了伦理问题。这些缺陷在研究期间持续存在，没有显著改善。在分析采用因素时，我们发现基准采用与作者知名度和代码可运行性相关，但与代码质量标准（如Pylint评分和可维护性）无关，这表明社区的基准选择并未奖励更高的编码标准。基于这些结果，我们识别出潜在的安全和可靠性问题。一些安全基准代码库公开暴露有害内容，例如成功的越狱响应，而没有任何伦理警告或访问控制，实际上充当了无防护的攻击资源。此外，当基准需要临时修改才能运行时，不同论文之间的下游安全评估可能无法比较。我们展示了这些具体后果的案例研究，并提出了一份针对性的检查清单，以帮助基准贡献者提高代码质量、文档和伦理实践。

Previous methods did not adequately measure these aspects, leading to issues with benchmark reliability and community adoption. This study introduces a comprehensive measurement approach that combines automated static analysis, human testing, and bibliometric analysis across 31 LLM safety benchmarks and a control group of 382 non-benchmark papers. The findings reveal significant deficiencies in benchmark repositories, with only 39% runnable without modification and a concerning lack of ethical considerations. The paper contributes by highlighting the disconnect between benchmark adoption and coding standards, identifying safety risks, and proposing a checklist for improving code quality and ethical practices in benchmark contributions. The methodology effectively demonstrates the need for better benchmarks to ensure reliable safety evaluations in LLM research.

The Great Pretender: A Stochasticity Problem in LLM Jailbreak
Authors: Jean-Philippe Monteuuis, Cong Chen, Jonathan Petit
First: 2026-05-14T06:05:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-14T06:05:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
"Oh-Oh, yes, I'm the great pretender. Pretending that I'm doing well. My need is such, I pretend too much..." summarizes the state in the area of jailbreak creation and evaluation. You find this method to generate adversarial attacks proposed by a reputable institution (e.g., BoN from Anthropic or Crescendo from Microsoft Research). However, this method does not deliver on the promise claimed in the paper despite having top ASR scores against industry-grade LLMs. You successfully generate the jailbreak prompts against your target (open) model. However, the generated jailbreak prompt works against the target model with a 50% consecutive success rate (5 out of 10 attempts) despite having an 80% ASR (on paper) on the latest closed-source model (with a guardrail system)! This observation leads us to think. First, Attack Success Rate (ASR), the primary metric for LLM jailbreak benchmarking, is not a stable quantity. Second, published ASR numbers are therefore systematically inflated and incomparable across papers. Therefore, we wonder "Why a successful jailbreak prompt does not perform consistently well against a target model on which the prompts have been optimized?". To answer this question, we study the impact of stochasticity not only during attack evaluation but also during attack generation. Our evaluation includes several jailbreak attacks, models (different sizes and providers), and judges. In addition, we propose a new metric and two new frameworks (CAS-eval and CAS-gen). Our evaluation framework, CAS-eval, shows that an attack can have an ASR drop of up to 30 percentage points when a jailbreak prompt needs to succeed on more than one attempt. Thankfully, our attack generation framework (CAS-gen) improves previous jailbreak methods and helps them recover this loss of 30 percentage points!
中文标题/摘要
标题：伟大的伪装者：LLM越狱中的随机性问题
"哦-哦，是的，我是伟大的伪装者。假装我做得很好。我的需求如此，我假装得太多……"总结了越狱创建和评估领域的现状。你发现了由一个知名机构（例如，Anthropic的BoN或微软研究院的Crescendo）提出的生成对抗攻击的方法。然而，尽管在行业级LLM上具有顶级的ASR分数，这种方法并没有兑现论文中所声称的承诺。你成功地针对目标（开放）模型生成了越狱提示。然而，生成的越狱提示在目标模型上的连续成功率为50%（10次尝试中有5次成功），尽管在最新的闭源模型（带有护栏系统）上在纸面上有80%的ASR！这一观察促使我们思考。首先，攻击成功率（ASR），作为LLM越狱基准测试的主要指标，并不是一个稳定的量。其次，发布的ASR数字因此系统性地被夸大，并且在不同论文之间不可比。因此，我们想知道“为什么成功的越狱提示在经过优化的目标模型上表现不一致良好？”为了回答这个问题，我们研究了随机性在攻击评估和攻击生成中的影响。我们的评估包括几种越狱攻击、模型（不同大小和提供者）和评审。此外，我们提出了一个新指标和两个新框架（CAS-eval和CAS-gen）。我们的评估框架CAS-eval显示，当越狱提示需要在多次尝试中成功时，攻击的ASR可能下降多达30个百分点。值得庆幸的是，我们的攻击生成框架（CAS-gen）改进了以前的越狱方法，并帮助它们恢复这30个百分点的损失！
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the inconsistencies in the effectiveness of jailbreak prompts for large language models (LLMs), highlighting that existing methods, such as those from reputable institutions, often report inflated Attack Success Rates (ASR) that do not translate into reliable performance. The authors identify that the primary issue lies in the stochastic nature of both attack generation and evaluation, which has not been adequately considered in prior research. To tackle these problems, the paper introduces two new frameworks: CAS-eval for evaluating attack performance and CAS-gen for generating more effective jailbreak prompts. The proposed methodologies demonstrate that ASR can drop significantly when prompts are tested for consecutive success, and CAS-gen effectively mitigates this issue, leading to improved performance in jailbreak attempts. The findings reveal that the new frameworks provide a more accurate assessment of jailbreak effectiveness, supporting the need for a reevaluation of existing benchmarks in this field.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLM）越狱提示的有效性不一致性，强调现有方法在纸面上虽然实现了高攻击成功率（ASR），但在实际应用中往往失败。以往的方法未能充分考虑攻击生成和评估的随机性，导致ASR指标被夸大，无法反映实际性能。本文通过提出一个新的评估框架（CAS-eval）和一个攻击生成框架（CAS-gen），考虑随机性，揭示在多次尝试中测试提示时ASR可能显著下降。所提出的方法显示出改进的性能，恢复了高达30个百分点的ASR损失，从而提供了对目标模型越狱有效性更可靠的评估。
Reducing the Safety Tax in LLM Safety Alignment with On-Policy Self-Distillation
Authors: Yu Fu, Longxuan Yu, Haz Sameen Shahgir, Zhipeng Wei, Hui Liu, N. Benjamin Erichson, Yue Dong
First: 2026-05-14T03:40:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-14T03:40:07+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety alignment often improves robustness to harmful queries at the cost of reasoning ability, a tradeoff known as the safety tax. A common cause is distributional mismatch: supervised fine-tuning trains the target model on safety demonstrations produced by humans, external models, or fixed self-generated traces, rather than on trajectories sampled from its own policy. We identify off-policy training mismatch as a second source of this tax and study on-policy self-distillation for safety alignment, which we call OPSA. The model generates its own rollouts and receives dense per-token KL supervision from a frozen teacher copy of itself conditioned on a privileged safety context. Because this teacher must be safer than the sampled student trajectory, we introduce \emph{teacher flip rate}: a criterion that measures how often a privileged context converts unsafe responses into safe ones. We use this signal to search for contexts that activate latent safety reasoning rather than merely elicit safe-looking demonstrations. Across two reasoning-model families and five model scales, OPSA achieves a stronger safety--reasoning tradeoff than off-policy self-distillation and external-teacher distillation under matched data and full-parameter fine-tuning, with the largest gains on smaller models (+8.85 points on R1-Distill-1.5B and +5.49 points on Qwen3-0.6B). The gains persist across training-set sizes and adaptive jailbreak evaluations. Token-level analyses further show that OPSA concentrates updates near early compliance-decision tokens, providing a mechanism for improving safety while preserving general reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过在线自蒸馏减少大语言模型安全对齐中的安全税
安全对齐通常在提高对有害查询的鲁棒性的同时牺牲推理能力，这种权衡被称为安全税。一个常见原因是分布不匹配：监督微调在由人类、外部模型或固定自生成轨迹产生的安全示例上训练目标模型，而不是在其自身策略采样的轨迹上。我们将离策略训练不匹配识别为这种税的第二个来源，并研究用于安全对齐的在线自蒸馏，称为OPSA。该模型生成自己的回滚，并从一个冻结的教师副本中接收每个标记的密集KL监督，该副本基于特权安全上下文进行条件化。由于这个教师必须比采样的学生轨迹更安全，我们引入了“教师翻转率”：一个衡量特权上下文将不安全响应转化为安全响应的频率的标准。我们利用这个信号寻找激活潜在安全推理的上下文，而不仅仅是引出看似安全的示例。在两个推理模型系列和五个模型规模中，OPSA在匹配数据和全参数微调下实现了比离策略自蒸馏和外部教师蒸馏更强的安全-推理权衡，在较小模型上获得了最大的增益（R1-Distill-1.5B上+8.85分，Qwen3-0.6B上+5.49分）。这些增益在训练集大小和自适应越狱评估中持续存在。标记级分析进一步表明，OPSA集中更新在早期合规决策标记附近，提供了一种在保持一般推理的同时提高安全性的机制。

This research addresses the challenge of safety alignment in large language models (LLMs), which often leads to a tradeoff between robustness to harmful queries and reasoning ability, termed the safety tax. Previous methods, such as off-policy self-distillation and external-teacher distillation, suffer from distributional mismatch and do not effectively leverage the model's own policy for safety training. The proposed approach, on-policy self-distillation for safety alignment (OPSA), mitigates these issues by allowing the model to generate its own rollouts and receive supervision from a frozen teacher model, thus enhancing safety reasoning. The paper contributes a novel criterion called teacher flip rate to evaluate the effectiveness of safety contexts and demonstrates that OPSA achieves a superior safety-reasoning balance compared to existing methods, with significant performance improvements on smaller models, achieving gains of +8.85 points on R1-Distill-1.5B and +5.49 points on Qwen3-0.6B, while maintaining robustness across various training conditions.

Quantifying LLM Safety Degradation Under Repeated Attacks Using Survival Analysis
Authors: Zvi Topol
First: 2026-05-13T01:26:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T01:26:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in a wide range of applications, yet remain vulnerable to adversarial jailbreak attacks that circumvent their safety guardrails. Existing evaluation frameworks typically report binary success/failure metrics, failing to capture the temporal dynamics of how attacks succeed under persistent adversarial pressure. This preliminary work proposes a novel evaluation framework that applies survival analysis techniques to characterize LLM jailbreak vuln`erability. Our approach models the time-to-jailbreak as a survival outcome, enabling estimation of hazard functions, survival curves, and risk factors associated with successful attacks. We evaluate three LLMs against a subset of prompts from the HarmBench dataset spanning three attack categories. Our analysis reveals that models exhibit distinct vulnerability profiles: while one model demonstrates rapid degradation under iterative attacks, the two other models show consistent moderate vulnerability. Our framework provides actionable insights for model and LLM application developers and establishes survival analysis as a rigorous methodology for LLM safety evaluation.

RACC: Representation-Aware Coverage Criteria for LLM Safety Testing
Authors: Zeming Wei, Zhixin Zhang, Chengcan Wu, Yihao Zhang, Xiaokun Luan, Meng Sun
First: 2026-02-02T16:20:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T03:47:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) face severe safety risks from jailbreak attacks, yet current safety testing largely relies on static datasets and lacks systematic criteria to evaluate test suite quality and adequacy. While coverage criteria have proven effective for smaller neural networks, they are impractical for LLMs due to computational overhead and the entanglement of safety-critical signals with irrelevant neuron activations. To address these issues, we propose RACC (Representation-Aware Coverage Criteria), a set of coverage criteria specialized for LLM safety testing. RACC first extracts safety representations from the LLM's hidden states using a small calibration set of harmful prompts, then measures test prompts' concept activations against these directions, and finally computes coverage through six criteria assessing both individual and compositional safety concept coverage. Experiments on multiple LLMs and safety benchmarks show that RACC reliably rewards high-quality jailbreak test suites while remaining insensitive to redundant or invalid inputs, which is a key distinction that neuron-level criteria fail to make. We further demonstrate RACC's practical value in two applications, including test suite prioritization and attack prompt sampling, and validate its generalization across diverse settings and configurations. Overall, RACC provides a scalable and principled foundation for coverage-guided LLM safety testing.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RACC：面向表示的LLM安全测试覆盖标准
大型语言模型（LLM）面临来自越狱攻击的严重安全风险，但当前的安全测试主要依赖静态数据集，缺乏系统化的标准来评估测试套件的质量和充分性。虽然覆盖标准在较小的神经网络中已被证明有效，但由于计算开销和安全关键信号与无关神经元激活的纠缠，它们在LLM中并不实用。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了RACC（面向表示的覆盖标准），这是一组专门针对LLM安全测试的覆盖标准。RACC首先使用一小组有害提示从LLM的隐藏状态中提取安全表示，然后根据这些方向测量测试提示的概念激活，最后通过六个标准计算覆盖，评估个体和组合安全概念的覆盖。对多个LLM和安全基准的实验表明，RACC可靠地奖励高质量的越狱测试套件，同时对冗余或无效输入保持不敏感，这是神经元级标准无法做到的关键区别。我们进一步展示了RACC在两个应用中的实际价值，包括测试套件优先级排序和攻击提示采样，并验证了其在不同设置和配置中的泛化能力。总体而言，RACC为覆盖引导的LLM安全测试提供了可扩展和原则性的基础。

FragBench: Cross-Session Attacks Hidden in Benign-Looking Fragments
Authors: Astha Mehta, Niruthiha Selvanayagam, Cedric Lam, Hengxu Li, Phuc-Nguyen Nguyen, Raymond Lee, Olivia McGoffin, My, Luong, Arthur Collé, Jamie Johnson, David Williams-King, Linh Le
First: 2026-05-10T21:06:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T21:06:48+00:00
Comments: preprint of submission
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
An attacker can split a malicious goal into sub-prompts that each look benign on their own and only become harmful in combination. Existing LLM safety benchmarks evaluate prompts one at a time, or across turns of a single chat, and so do not look for a malicious signal spread across separate sessions with no shared context. We build FragBench, a benchmark drawn from 24 real-world cyber-incident campaigns, which keeps the full attack trail: the multi-fragment kill chain, the per-fragment safety-judge verdicts, sandboxed execution traces, and a matched set of benign cover sessions. FragBench splits this trail into two paired tasks: an adversarial rewriter that hardens fragments against a single-turn safety judge (FragBench Attack), and a graph-based user-level detector trained on the resulting interactions (FragBench Defense). The single-turn judge is near chance on the released corpus by construction, but four GNN variants and three classical-ML baselines all recover the cross-session feature, reaching aggregate event-level F1 = 0.88-0.96. Defending against fragmented LLM misuse therefore requires modeling the cross-session interaction graph, rather than isolated prompts. Our generator, rewriter, sandbox harness, and detector are released at https://github.com/LidaSafety/fragbench.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FragBench：隐藏在看似良性片段中的跨会话攻击
攻击者可以将恶意目标拆分为看似良性的子提示，这些子提示单独看时无害，但组合在一起时会变得有害。现有的LLM安全基准一次评估一个提示，或在单个聊天的多个回合中评估，因此未能寻找跨会话的恶意信号，这些会话之间没有共享上下文。我们构建了FragBench，这是一个基于24个真实网络事件活动的基准，保留了完整的攻击轨迹：多片段杀伤链、每个片段的安全评判结果、沙箱执行痕迹，以及一组匹配的良性覆盖会话。FragBench将这一轨迹分为两个配对任务：一个对抗重写器，旨在增强片段对单回合安全评判的抵抗力（FragBench Attack），以及一个基于图的用户级检测器，训练于结果交互（FragBench Defense）。单回合评判在发布的语料库中几乎是随机的，但四种GNN变体和三种经典机器学习基线都恢复了跨会话特征，达到聚合事件级F1 = 0.88-0.96。因此，防御碎片化的LLM误用需要建模跨会话交互图，而不是孤立的提示。我们的生成器、重写器、沙箱工具和检测器已在https://github.com/LidaSafety/fragbench发布。

This article addresses the challenge of detecting cross-session attacks in large language models (LLMs), where malicious prompts are split into benign-looking fragments that only become harmful when combined. Previous methods have focused on evaluating prompts in isolation or within a single chat session, failing to capture the malicious signals that can emerge across different sessions without shared context. The proposed approach, FragBench, introduces a benchmark that retains the complete attack trail from real-world cyber incidents and divides it into two tasks: an adversarial rewriter to fortify fragments against single-turn safety assessments and a graph-based user-level detector trained on the interactions. The paper demonstrates that existing single-turn judges perform poorly, while their method achieves an aggregate event-level F1 score between 0.88 and 0.96 using various graph neural network and classical machine learning models, indicating that effective defense against fragmented LLM misuse necessitates understanding cross-session interactions rather than treating prompts in isolation.
